                         APPENDIX
                                        BACKGROUND

Metro Development is proposing to develop a site with single family homes in the City of
Powell. The site is located on the south side of Home Road west of Steitz Road. Figure 1 shows
the location of the site. There are two locations of proposed access: one on Home Road and one
to Steitz Road via Hunter's Bend. The Home Road right of way is in the jurisdiction of the
Delaware County Engineers Office. Figure 2 shows the proposed site layout.

As part of the access, a traffic study is required The Delaware County Engineer's Office (DCEO)
is the reviewing agency for the traffic study. Traffic Engineering Services, Inc. has been
retained by the developer to perform the TIS. A pre meeting for the study was held with the
DCEO on April 15, 2013. The scope of the TIS was discussed at this meeting and a formal
memo of understanding (MOU) dated April, 22 2013 was submitted to the DCEO. A copy of the
MOU is in the Appendix.

                                     EXISTING CONDITIONS
The following is a list of the traffic control at the study area intersections:

                        yHome Road & Site Access - Unsignalized
                        ySteitz Road & Hunter's Bend (Access to Site) - Unsignalized
                        yHome Road & Steitz Road - Unsignalized
                        yHome Road & Sawmill Parkway - Signalized
                        ySteitz Road & Rutherford Road ­ Unsignalized
                        ySawmill Parkway & Rutherford Road - Signalized

Table 1 shows the speed limit and classification of each roadway in the study area.

                                                                        Delaware County
                         Street                    Speed Limit          Throughfare Plan
                                                                          Classification
                       Home Road                      55 mph              Major Arterial

                       Steitz Road                    55 mph              Major Collector

                      Hunters Bend                    25 mph                  Local

                     Rutherford Road                  45 mph              Minor Collector

                    Sawmill Parkway                   45 mph              Major Arterial
                          TABLE 1 ­ Summary of Roadway Designations


As part of the project, new turning movement counts (7-9 AM & 4-6 PM) were taken at the five
existing intersections in the study area. The count reports are in the Appendix. In addition, 24
hour machine counts were taken on Home Road west of Steitz Road, Rutherford Road east of
Steitz Road, and Steitz Road south of Home Road. The count reports for these counts are also in
the Appendix. It is noted that on all counts the times 7-8 AM and 5-6 PM were considered in the
study.

               Home Road Site (S of Home; W of Steitz) Traffic Impact Study - 3
                            PROJECTED SITE TRAFFIC

Trip Generation
The site traffic was computed using Trip Generation, 9th Edition, published by the Institute of
Transportation Engineers (ITE). The land use is "Single Family Detached Housing" (ITE Code
#210). Though there are currently 119 units proposed, 120 units were assumed in the study to
be conservative. Table 2 shows a summary of the trip generation calculations.

Trip Distribution
Per the MOU, the following distribution was approved by the DCEO for use in the study:

              y25% west on Home Road at Site Access
              y31% east on Home Road at Site Access
               3% north on Sawmill Parkway
                16% east on Home Road (east of Sawmill Parkway)
               12% south on Sawmill Parkway
              y14% north on Steitz Road at Hunters Bend
                2% east on Home Road/north on Sawmill Parkway
                12% east on Home Road (east of Sawmill Parkway)
              y30% south on Steitz Road at Hunters Bend
               15% west on Rutherford Road
               15% east on Rutherford Road/south on Sawmill Parkway

                               2014 AND 2024 TRAFFIC

A 10 year horizon is required for the traffic study. Opening day is 2014 which makes the design
year 2024. The Mid Ohio Regional Planning Commission (MORPC) provided compounded per
year growth rates for use in the TIS. The correspondence from MORPC is in the Appendix. The
following are the growth rates and corresponding factors:

                                           Compounded Per Year Growth Rate
       Segment                             (BaseYear: 2014 Factor, 2024 Factor)
       All (Except Hunters Bend)                 4% (1.04, 1.539)

It is noted that the growth rate was not applied to Hunters Bend movements since the existing
streets are basically developed. Figure 3 and 4 show all components for the 2014 traffic.
Figures 5 and 6 show all components of the 2024 traffic. To assist with the review, exhibits
showing the 2014 and 2024 `No Build' volumes have been provided in the Appendix.

                                    TRAFFIC ANALYSES

Turn Lane Warrant Analysis
Left Turn Lanes ­ According to the TIS Standards, there are three criteria to examine to
determine if left turn lanes are warranted at the site access. The first criterion is the procedure
found in the State Highway Access Management Manual (AMM) published by ODOT. The
second criterion is on roadways classified as Major or Minor Arterials with speeds greater than
40 MPH. The third criterion is on on major collector with speeds greater than 40 MPH and more
than 10 left turning vehicles during the peak hour for full build-out of the development. The
graphs from the AMM is in the Appendix. Table 2 includes a summary of the results of the left
turn lane warrants.

Right Turn Lanes - Per TIS Standards, the procedure for determining whether a right turn lane
is required is according to the procedures found in the AMM. The results show that a right turn
lane is not warranted for the site. The graphs from the AMM are in the Appendix. Table 2
includes a summary of the results of the right turn lane warrants.

              Home Road Site (S of Home; W of Steitz) Traffic Impact Study - 10
Signalized Capacity Analyses
Signalized capacity analyses were performed at the signalized intersections in the study area. In
the capacity analyses, delays are computed which correspond to a Level of Service (LOS) "A"
through "F". Typically, Level of Service (LOS) "D" or above is considered an acceptable LOS.
Since driver expectations are different for various types of traffic control, there are different LOS
criteria for unsignalized intersections versus signalized intersections. LOS criteria for signalized
intersections are shown in Table 2.

                     Level of Service                Delay Range (seconds/vehicle)
                            A                < 10
                            B                > 10 and < 20
                            C                > 20 and < 35
                            D                > 35 and < 55
                            E                > 55 and < 80
                            F                > 80
                                        Source: Highway Capacity Manual 2010
                  Table 4 - Level of Service Criteria for Signalized Intersections
The following comprises the background of the signalized capacity analysis:
  HCS 2010 6.41 was used to perform the analysis.
  The existing intersection Peak Hour Factor (PHF) was applied.
  Right Turns on Red (RTOR) were not assumed in the analysis.
  Existing lane configuration was used as the base condition.
  The signals are not coordinated.
  The revision to the existing signal timing was at Sawmill Parkway & Home Road and
  included the following:
       -Increase the maximum time on EB and WB through phases from 35 seconds to 40
       seconds.
       -Increase the maximum time on NB LT phase from 12 seconds to 18 seconds.
  The improvements identified for the 2024 `No Build' were as follows:
       Sawmill Parkway & Home Road
       -Build NB Dual left turn lane. (Receiving lane would be needed on WB Home Road).
       -Northbound left turn signal phasing changed to protected only operation.
       -Build EB Right turn lane and allow protected turn phase to run concurrently with
       northbound left turn phase.
       Sawmill Parkway & Rutherford Road
       -Increase maximum time for EB-WB from 15 seconds to 30 seconds.
       -Reduced maximum time for NB-SB from 80 seconds to 70 seconds

Table 5 shows a summary of the results of the signalized capacity analyses. The HCS 2010
reports are in the Appendix.

                                      CONCLUSIONS

2014 and 2024 `No Build' and `Build' volumes were developed for use in signal warrant
analysis (where specified), turn lane warrant analysis, signalized capacity analyses and turn lane
length calculations. The following is a summary of the conclusions for each time period.

                                      Existing Condition

       Sawmill Parkway & Home Road
           Analysis of existing timing resulted in the following timing revisions:
                   -Increase the maximum time on EB and WB through phases from 35
                   seconds to 40 seconds.
                   -Increase the maximum time on NB LT phase from 12 seconds to 18
                   seconds.

       Sawmill Parkway & Rutherford Road
           No timing revisions.

                                        2014 `No Build'

       Home Road & Steitz Road
           A westbound left turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 345'
           which includes the diverging taper.
           An eastbound right turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 345'
           which includes the diverging taper.

       Steitz Road & Hunters Bend
             A northbound left turn lane is warranted based on the criteria that Steitz Road is
             a Major Collector with a speed over 40 MPH and there are greater than 10 left
             turning vehicles. The length of the lane would be 345' which includes the
             diverging taper.

       Rutherford Road & Steitz Road
            An eastbound left turn lane is not warranted.
            A westbound right turn lane is not warranted.

       Sawmill Parkway & Home Road
           The intersection will operate at an acceptable Level of Service.
           The existing northbound left turn lane is approximately 565' long. The lane
           would need to be 600' (Maximum per L&D Manual) including diverging taper to
           meet the standard. Note that the offset distance of the lane was ignored in the
           calculation of the length.
           The existing eastbound left turn lane accommodates the traffic.
           The existing southbound left turn lane accommodates the traffic.

       Sawmill Parkway & Rutherford Road
           The intersection will operate at an acceptable Level of Service.

              Home Road Site (S of Home; W of Steitz) Traffic Impact Study - 14
       The existing northbound left turn lane is approximately 285' long. The lane
       would need to be 343' including diverging taper to meet the standard. Note that
       the offset distance of the lane was ignored in the calculation of the length.

                                 2014 `Build'

Home Road & Prop. Site Access
    A westbound left turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 345'
    which includes the diverging taper.
    An eastbound right turn lane is not warranted.

Home Road & Steitz Road
    Same as 2014 `No Build': A westbound left turn lane is warranted. The length
    of the lane would be 345' which includes the diverging taper.
    Same as 2014 `No Build': An eastbound right turn lane is warranted. The
    length of the lane would be 345' which includes the diverging taper.

Steitz Road & Hunters Bend
      Same as 2014 `No Build': A northbound left turn lane is warranted based on the
      criteria that Steitz Road is a Major Collector with a speed over 40 MPH and there
      are greater than 10 left turning vehicles. The length of the lane would be 345'
      which includes the diverging taper.

Rutherford Road & Steitz Road
     An eastbound left turn lane is not warranted.
     A westbound right turn lane is not warranted.

Sawmill Parkway & Home Road
    The intersection will operate at an acceptable Level of Service.
    Same as 2014 `No Build': The existing northbound left turn lane is
    approximately 565' long. The lane would need to be 600' (Maximum per L&D
    Manual) including diverging taper to meet the standard. Note that the offset
    distance of the lane was ignored in the calculation of the length.
    Same as 2014 `No Build': The existing eastbound left turn lane accommodates
    the traffic.
    Same as 2014 `No Build': The existing southbound left turn lane accommodates
    the traffic.

Sawmill Parkway & Rutherford Road
    The intersection will operate at an acceptable Level of Service.
    The existing northbound left turn lane is approximately 285' long. The lane
    would need to be 393' including diverging taper to meet the standard which is 50
    feet longer than the 2014 `No Build'. Note that the offset distance of the lane was
    ignored in the calculation of the length.

                                2024 `No Build'

Home Road & Steitz Road
    A westbound left turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 345'
    which includes the diverging taper.
    An eastbound right turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 345'
    which includes the diverging taper.

Steitz Road & Hunters Bend
      A northbound left turn lane is warranted based on the criteria that Steitz Road is
      a Major Collector with a speed over 40 MPH and there are greater than 10 left
      turning vehicles. The length of the lane would be 345' which includes the
      diverging taper.

Rutherford Road & Steitz Road
     An eastbound left turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 243'
     which includes the diverging taper.
     A westbound right turn lane is not warranted.

Sawmill Parkway & Home Road
    The intersection will not operate at an acceptable Level of Service. The
    following improvements are needed to bring the intersection to LOS D:
            -Build NB dual left turn lane which would include a sufficient length.
            westbound receiving lane on the west leg of the intersection. The
            development of the dual lanes would be per ODOT L&D Manual 401-12
            and would require a 600 foot distance to develop the lanes.
            -The northbound left turn signal phasing would be changed to protected
            only operation.
            -Build EB Right turn lane and allow protected turn phase to run
            concurrently with northbound left turn phase. The length of the eastbound
            right turn lane would be 556' which includes the diverging taper.
    The existing eastbound left turn lane accommodates the traffic.
    The existing southbound left turn lane accommodates the traffic.

Sawmill Parkway & Rutherford Road
    The intersection will operate at an acceptable Level of Service with the
    following timing adjustments:
            -Increase maximum time for EB-WB from 15 seconds to 30 seconds.
            -Reduced maximum time for NB-SB from 80 seconds to 70 seconds
    The existing northbound left turn lane is approximately 285' long. The lane
    would need to be 468' including diverging taper to meet the standard. Note that
    the offset distance of the lane was ignored in the calculation of the length.

    A westbound left turn lane is warranted. The length of the lane would be 345'

for calculating turn lane lengths does not account for the amount of green time or opportunity to
turn right on red. If mitigation or a contribution will be required for these, additional analyses
may need to be performed.

           No Improvements
